# Dutch Football Club Data

This file contains structured data for Dutch football clubs across different leagues. The data is organized by league tier and includes club details such as location, stadium, and other relevant information.

## Template

### Eredivisie (Tier 1)
```markdown
- **Club Name**: 
  - City: 
  - Stadium: 
  - Capacity: 
  - Founded: 
  - Colors: 
  - Rivals: 
  - Notes:
```

### Eerste Divisie (Tier 2)

```markdown
- **Club Name**: 
  - City: 
  - Stadium: 
  - Capacity: 
  - Founded: 
  - Colors: 
  - Rivals: 
  - Notes:
```

- **Kit**: Home / Away colors (🟡 Yellow, 🔴 Red, ⚫ Black, ⚪ White, 🔵 Blue, 🟢 Green, 🟠 Orange)
- **Value**: Approximate market value in millions
- **Rep**: Club reputation (★ to ★★★★★)

  - Focus on local talent development
  - Stadiums with 500-600 capacity
- **Season Structure**: 26 matchdays, home and away matches on Sundays

| 4 | PEC Zwolle -21 | PEC Zwolle | Sportpark Zuid | 1,000 | 🔵⚪ / ⚫🔵 | Development |
| 5 | Willem II -21 | Willem II | Sportpark De Wieen | 1,000 | 🔴⚪ / ⚫🔴 | Development |
| 6 | De Graafschap -21 | De Graafschap | De Vijverberg (B) | 1,000 | 🔵⚪ / ⚫🔵 | Development |
| 7 | Go Ahead Eagles -21 | Go Ahead Eagles | De Adelaarshorst (B) | 1,000 | 🟡⚫ / ⚫🟡 | Development |
| 8 | SC Cambuur -21 | SC Cambuur | Cambuurstadion (B) | 1,000 | 🟡🔵 / 🔵⚫ | Development |

**Notes**:
- **Parallel to**: Derde Divisie (same level in pyramid)
- **Promotion**: Top team may be promoted to Tweede Divisie (if not a B-team already in Eerste Divisie)
- **Relegation**: B-teams relegated from Tweede Divisie join this league
- **Rules**:
  - Maximum of 3 outfield players and 1 goalkeeper over 21 allowed
  - Cannot be promoted to Eerste Divisie (highest level for B-teams)
  - Serve as development teams for parent clubs

  - No relegation (bottom of U21 pyramid)
- **Rules**:
  - Same age restrictions as other O21 divisions (max 3 outfield + 1 GK over 21)
  - Teams can be promoted to O21 Divisie 2 but not directly to senior leagues
  - Focus on U21 development with limited overage players
  - Matches focus on player development over results

### O21 Divisie 1 (Top U21 League) - Fourth Tier

| # | Club | City | Stadium | Capacity | Kit (H/A) | Board Expectation |
|---|------|------|---------|----------|-----------|-------------------|
| 1 | AFC '34 -21 | Weesp | Sportpark De Hogewey | 1,000 | 🟡⚫ / ⚫🟡 | Development |
| 2 | Alphense Boys -21 | Alphen aan den Rijn | Sportpark de Bijlen | 1,000 | 🟡🔵 / 🔵⚫ | Development |
| 3 | DEM -21 | Haarlem | Sportpark de Molenwijk | 1,000 | 🔴⚪ / ⚪🔴 | Development |
| 4 | HHC Hardenberg -21 | Hardenberg | Sportpark De Boshoek (B) | 1,000 | 🟡⚫ / ⚫🟡 | Development |
| 5 | Hollandia -21 | Tuitjenhorn | Sportpark de Blauwe Berg | 1,000 | 🟢⚪ / ⚪🟢 | Development |
| 6 | HFC -21 | Haarlem | Sportpark Spanjaardlaan (B) | 1,000 | 🔴⚪ / ⚪🔴 | Development |
| 7 | Quick Boys -21 | Katwijk | Sportpark Nieuw Zuid (B) | 1,000 | 🟡⚫ / ⚫🟡 | Development |
| 8 | Zeeburgia -21 | Amsterdam | Sportpark Drieburg | 1,000 | 🟡🔵 / 🔵⚫ | Development |

**Notes**:
- **Level**: Three tiers below O21 Divisie 1 (Parallel to Tweede Klasse level)
- **Promotion/Relegation**:
  - Top team promotes to O21 Divisie 3
  - No relegation (bottom of U21 pyramid)
- **Rules**:
  - Same age restrictions as other O21 divisions (max 3 outfield + 1 GK over 21)
  - Teams can be promoted to O21 Divisie 3 but not directly to senior leagues
  - Strong emphasis on technical development and sportsmanship
  - Matches focus on player development over results
